### 11. 面向对象的科技信息图表模板

**Author**: [Edraak Tech | إدراك تِك](https://x.com/EdraakTechAi)  **Date**: 2026-02-24  **Language**: en

> 一个模板提示，用于创建任何对象的科技信息图，采用 45 度等距 3D 透视，结合照片级真实感、黑色墨水注释以及用于功能/流程的颜色编码箭头。

![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512625_1omobh_HB4jNMqXQAAQHJE.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512780_i7a0s3_HB4jNLvWgAALsmW.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001512653_wu5r6i_HB4jNL1XkAAa_CV.jpg)
![面向对象的科技信息图表模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772001514012_n92c2t_HB4jNMYWMAEDohe.jpg)

```
Create a technical infographic of {argument name="object name" default="[OBJECT NAME]"} with a 45-degree isometric 3D perspective showing the device slightly tilted to reveal depth and dimension.
Combine a realistic photoreal render with black ink technical annotations on pure white background. Include:
Key component labels with color-coded callout boxes Internal component visibility through transparent/cutaway sections
Measurements, dimensions, and precise scale markers Material callouts and quantities 
Color-coded arrows for function/flow: RED (power/battery), BLUE (data/connectivity), ORANGE (thermal/processor), GREEN (sensors/haptics)
Simple schematics or cross-sectional diagrams where relevant 
Place “OBJECT NAME” title in a hand-drawn technical box (top-left corner).
Style: Black linework (technical pen/architectural), sketched but precise. Object remains clearly visible. Educational museum-exhibit vibe. Clean composition, balanced negative space.
Perspective: Isometric 3D angle—tilted to show depth, dimension, and internal architecture dramatically. Like a professional product teardown or engineering manual.
Colors: ~10–15% accent density. Black dominant. White background.
Output: 1080×1080, ultra-crisp, social-feed optimized.
```

![Madelyn Cline 网球场补水肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771915001092_poyzu6_HB4Df8nWgAAHYq9.jpg)
![Madelyn Cline 网球场补水肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771915001106_c4cy6h_HB4Df8sXIAAEsdR.jpg)
![Madelyn Cline 网球场补水肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771915001247_t1ngz4_HB4Df8lXIAAkg9I.jpg)

```
Madelyn Cline mid-20s, sun-kissed tanned skin with post-match glow and light perspiration, long dark brown hair in high ponytail slightly damp and messy from intense play, distinctive features with confident expression, minimal natural makeup showing real skin.

Curvy hourglass athletic build, skin glistening from workout.

Wearing white pleated tennis skirt, white fitted athletic tank top damp from sweat and water clinging to body showing natural silhouette, white ankle socks and sneakers.

Standing court-side, drinking from water bottle tilted back, water bottle raised to lips, some water spilling down onto chest and soaking into already damp tank top, one hand on hip, back naturally arched, confident expression looking at camera while hydrating.
```

```
A stylized medieval fantasy village at morning featuring a Village Inn with carved wooden balcony railings and dormer windows, a Timber-Framed Village Cottage built on a stone foundation base with exposed timber beams and plaster wall panels, a Market Square Shopfront with timber awning frame and striped fabric canopy, a Guard Barracks with buttress supports and arrow slit windows, a Stone Watchtower with circular tower windows and crenellation detail, and a Noble Manor House with multiple steep shingled roofs and decorative roof finials. The Reflective Water Body remains unobstructed, with activity limited to the Wooden Dock Platform and shoreline only. Dense pine forest clusters and broadleaf village trees frame the scene, rounded shrubs edge the cobblestone paths, lantern posts and wooden benches define gathering areas.

Style:
Cinematic stylized fantasy medieval village, warm golden morning sunlight, long soft shadows, clean blue sky illumination, subtle volumetric light rays, painterly materials, softened stone and wood textures, vibrant but controlled color grading, rounded stylized forms, balanced exposure, atmospheric clarity, cozy environmental realism, high-end game environment quality

Camera:
```

**Author**: [𝐌](https://x.com/Strength04_X)  **Date**: 2026-02-23  **Language**: en

> 一个可复用的提示模板，用于生成任何指定对象的科技信息图。该信息图以 45 度等距 3D 视角呈现，结合了逼真的渲染效果、黑色墨水技术注释、彩色标注和示意图。

```
“Create a technical infographic of {argument name="object" default="OBJECT"} with a 45-degree isometric 3D perspective showing the device slightly tilted to reveal depth and dimension.
Combine a realistic photoreal render with black ink technical annotations on pure white background. Include:
Key component labels with color-coded callout boxes
Internal component visibility through transparent/cutaway sections
Measurements, dimensions, and precise scale markers
Material callouts and quantities
Color-coded arrows for function/flow: RED (power/battery), BLUE (data/connectivity), ORANGE (thermal/processor), GREEN (sensors/haptics)
Simple schematics or cross-sectional diagrams where relevant

Place “OBJECT” title in a hand-drawn technical box (top-left corner).
Style: Black linework (technical pen/architectural), sketched but precise. Object remains clearly visible. Educational museum-exhibit vibe. Clean composition, balanced negative space.
Perspective: Isometric 3D angle—tilted to show depth, dimension, and internal architecture dramatically. Like a professional product teardown or engineering manual.
Colors: ~10-15% accent density. Black dominant. White background.
Output: 1080×1080, ultra-crisp, social-feed optimized.”
```

```
{
  "vibe_title_en": "Obsidian Ritual",
  "master_prompt": "A hyper-realistic, monochrome close-up portrait of The Protagonist, styled in avant-garde tribal brutalism. ### 65. 用于对象标注的技术信息图叠加
```

**Author**: [Edraak Tech | إدراك تِك](https://x.com/EdraakTechAi)  **Date**: 2026-02-23  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的提示模板，旨在通过将物体的真实照片与技术性、建筑风格的注释叠加相结合，生成信息图图像。它指定标签、内部轮廓、测量和功能箭头仅使用白色背景上的黑线，以营造一种教育性的工程手册美学。

![用于对象标注的技术信息图叠加](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771915001456_ihgqiy_HBzijzrXkAAFkKT.jpg)
![用于对象标注的技术信息图叠加](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771915001462_fzqkfc_HBzijznXMAEkxUV.jpg)

```
Create an infographic image of {argument name="object" default="[OBJECT]"}, combining a realistic photograph or photorealistic rendering of the object with an overlay of technical annotations placed directly on top.
Use black ink line drawings and text (in the style of a technical pen / architectural sketch) on a clean white studio background, including:
• Labels on key components
• Internal outlines in cutaway or cross-section view
• Measurement, dimension, and scale markers
• Material and quantity designations
• Arrows indicating function, force, or flow (air, sound, power, pressure)
• Simple diagrams or cross-sections where appropriate
Place the title {argument name="object title" default="[OBJECT]"} in a box with hand-drawn technical notes in one of the corners.
Style and layout rules:
• The real object remains clearly visible under the annotations
• Annotations look schematic, technical, and architectural
• Clear composition with balanced negative space
• Educational atmosphere resembling a museum exhibition or engineering manual.
Visual style:
Minimalist technical illustration aesthetics, black lines over realistic images, crisp but slightly hand-drawn.
Color palette:
White background, only black annotation lines and text. No colors.
Output:
1080x1080 resolution, very sharp image, optimized for social media, no watermarks.
```

[[White Background]] [[Template Prompt]]

### 66. Nano Banana Pro 的奢华镜面自拍提示词

**Author**: [Ella](https://x.com/ellas_pics)  **Date**: 2026-02-23  **Language**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 提示，旨在生成一张年轻女性在豪华深色大理石浴室中拍摄的超逼真垂直镜面自拍照。该提示详细说明了拍摄对象的夸张沙漏身材、姿势、服装（豹纹紧身胸衣和迷你裙）、灯光和相机设置，以达到时尚杂志摄影的品质。

![Nano Banana Pro 的奢华镜面自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771914992049_vzvuxb_HBzgykhXQAAPQ7E.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "A vertical straight-on mirror selfie of a young woman with long wavy blonde highlighted hair in a luxurious dark marble bathroom at night.",
    "body": {
      "physique": "A slim, exaggerated hourglass figure with a curvaceous bust and extremely narrow waist accentuated by the corset silhouette.",
      "pose": "Standing directly facing the mirror head-on, body fully square to the mirror, taking a selfie with a gold iPhone held straight up at face level. Subtle weight shift to one hip for natural posture.",
      "features": "Long wavy blonde highlighted hair worn down. Full lips, defined brows, glamorous makeup. Flawless, tattoo-free skin."
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "outfit": "A matching leopard print strapless corset top and ruched leopard print mini skirt with a midriff cutout between the two pieces."
    }
  },
  "pose_action": "Standing perfectly square and straight-on to the mirror, phone held centered at face height, capturing a direct full front-facing mirror selfie with no body angle or rotation.",
  "scene": {
    "environment": "A high-end hotel or luxury penthouse bathroom at night.",
    "elements": "Dark brown and black marble walls, large ornate gold-framed mirror centered on the wall, glass shower enclosure with gold fixtures visible in background, warm recessed ceiling lighting.",
    "composition": "Vertical straight-on mirror selfie capturing full body from mid-thigh to top of head, subject perfectly centered in the mirror frame, phone and hand visible reflected in mirror at face level."
  },
  "lighting": {
    "setup": "Warm ambient evening lighting from recessed ceiling lights, supplemented by soft glow of the phone screen illuminating her face from the front.",
    "details": "Warm golden tones reflect off the marble walls. Even front-facing illumination with soft highlights on hair and skin. No harsh shadows. Mirror reflection is sharp and clear."
  },
  "camera": {
    "technical": "Ultra-realistic straight-on mirror selfie photograph in 9:16 aspect ratio. Sharp focus on face and full outfit. Subject centered in frame. Editorial fashion photography quality, highly detailed."
  }
}
```

### 86. 赛博投影仪数字美女肖像提示 (JSON 格式)

**Author**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1)  **Date**: 2026-02-21  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 格式 Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成一张超高分辨率、电影级美学肖像，描绘一位女性，其面部和身体上映射着绿色的数字投影，强调照片级真实感、低调照明和正确的投影物理效果。

![赛博投影仪数字美女肖像提示 (JSON 格式)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741712921_n6eig7_HBtgxStXYAE3eAJ.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "cyber_projector_numbers_beauty_portrait",
      "version": "v1.0_GREEN_NUMBERS_PROJECTION_BEAUTY",
      "priority": "highest",
      "language": "en"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "text_to_image",
      "notes": "Create a photoreal cinematic beauty portrait of an adult woman with green numeric projections mapped across her face, neck, shoulders, and chest. The projection must look physically correct (wraps around facial contours), with soft falloff and slight blur at edges. Dark background with faint out-of-focus green digits. Moody, low-key lighting. No text, no watermark."
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "render_style": "cinematic_techno_editorial",
      "sharpness": "filmic_crisp",
      "grain": "subtle_35mm",
      "color_grading": "green_on_black_low_key"
    },
    "scene": {
      "environment": "dark studio, faint bokeh of green digits in the background",
      "lighting": "primary light is the projector (green digits), minimal soft fill from camera-left, deep shadows",
      "mood": "mysterious, cyber, intimate"
    },
    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",
      "pose": "3/4 portrait, head slightly tilted, eyes looking sideways past camera",
      "expression": "calm, intense, enigmatic",
      "hair": "long dark hair, sleek and natural",
      "makeup": "clean editorial skin, subtle shimmer on eyelids, soft liner, natural glossy lips",
      "skin_texture": "natural pores, realistic highlights"
    },
    "camera": {
      "camera_body": "ARRI Alexa Mini",
      "lens": "85mm prime",
      "aperture": "f/2.0",
      "focus": "sharp on eyes and lips, projection still readable, background bokeh"
    },
    "projection_details": {
      "content": "random green digits (0-9) and simple symbols",
      "behavior": "wraps on cheekbones, nose bridge, jawline, collarbones",
      "quality": "slight projector softness, realistic spill light on skin"
    },
    "negative_prompt": "text, watermark, logo, letters, neon signs, cartoon, anime, CGI look, plastic skin, over-smoothing, distorted face, extra limbs, extra fingers, deformed hands, incorrect projection physics, flat overlay, low resolution, heavy HDR"
  }
}
```

![坚固矿业聚落的收藏级微缩立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741700290_rwd8vz_HBtATw3bgAADXCz.jpg)

```
SCENE:
A rugged mining settlement built into a jungle-covered volcanic slope with wooden platforms, drilling towers, and rope lifts. Tiny workers guide carts along narrow tracks while monkeys climb vines and dense foliage surrounds the machinery.

When generating or inventing a scene, prioritize architectural and cultural diversity and intentionally vary the environment type, building styles, historical inspiration, regional influence, and settlement purpose so each generated miniature feels visually distinct and not a repetition of common village, temple, garden, or plaza layouts.
Ensure the architecture organizes around a natural central hub so structures cluster with believable spatial gravity, forming a cohesive miniature settlement with denser core structures and supporting elements arranged outward. Arrange the layout as a compact, layered, interconnected district filling the platform naturally without empty gaps. Ensure the entire environment clearly reads as a small handcrafted tabletop collectible model, with miniature-scale architecture and compressed model-world proportions rather than life-sized buildings.
STYLE:
Frame the camera at a stable product-display distance so the entire collectible diorama remains clearly visible with comfortable margins, avoiding close cinematic crops or environmental perspective shots. Render as a premium stylized 3D collectible miniature diorama on a fully visible, centered self-contained display base, shown from a slightly elevated 3/4 tabletop angle against a clean neutral studio gradient background. Maintain collectible figurine scale and clean display presentation.
All elements should appear sculpted from smooth matte ceramic, painted resin, or stylized polymer with rounded edges, simplified geometry, and slightly exaggerated toy-like proportions. Keep surfaces clean and intentionally stylized. Avoid fingerprints, rough handmade textures, workshop scenes, macro photography depth-of-field, or photoreal clay imperfections.
Use soft professional studio product lighting: gentle global illumination, warm key light, soft ambient bounce, controlled shadows, and optional warm interior window glow.
Render any water or translucent materials as poured clear resin with smooth transparency, subtle reflections, soft internal depth, and slightly thick stylized edges.
Include small environmental details but keep everything cohesive, simplified, and sculptural. Prioritize clean stylized modeling over photorealistic texture detail.
Overall intent: premium collectible miniature, stylized 3D marketplace presentation, cozy whimsical mood, smooth sculpt clarity, controlled studio rendering, avoid real-world photography aesthetics.
aspect ratio 4:3
```

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供一个高度详细的提示，用于创作一个超现实的平面构图，其中标志完全由压花和干叶构成。该构图置于有纹理的手工纸上，强调柔和的自然光、精致的阴影以及艺术、质朴的氛围。

```
アップロードしたロゴを、押し花と乾燥した葉だけで形作り、テクスチャのある手漉き紙の上に丁寧に配置した、超リアルなフラットレイ構成を作成してください。ロゴの形状は、様々な自然の花びら、茎、植物の要素から正確に構成されています。片側からの柔らかな自然光、繊細な影、落ち着いた芸術的な雰囲気。アースカラーのトーン、繊細なテクスチャ、そしてリアリティのためにわずかな不完全さを加えています。印刷されたロゴは使用せず、有機的な素材のみで形を形作っています。
```

### 104. Vlog 风格时尚视频拍摄

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-21  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个视频（使用基于 Nano Banana Pro 图像的 Google Veo 3.1），该视频模仿逼真、高质量的夜间室内 Vlog 拍摄。该提示指定了摄像机角度、稳定的构图、逼真的灯光、轻松的表情，并包含适合时尚 Vlog 的对话和背景音乐。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Natural Lighting]] [[Candid Expression]] [[Lifestyle Content]]

### 113. 赛博朋克城市街区收藏级立体模型

![赛博朋克城市街区收藏级立体模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771655056348_e4b5y9_HBoK5MgbMAA7L0D.jpg)

```
SCENE:
A layered cyberpunk city block combining low historic structures at ground level with towering neon skyscrapers rising above, connected by bridges, cables, and stacked infrastructure.
STYLE:
Render as a premium stylized 3D collectible miniature diorama on a fully visible, centered self-contained display base, shown from a slightly elevated 3/4 tabletop angle against a clean neutral studio gradient background. Maintain collectible figurine scale and clean display presentation.
All elements should appear sculpted from smooth matte ceramic, painted resin, or stylized polymer with rounded edges, simplified geometry, and slightly exaggerated toy-like proportions. Keep surfaces clean and intentionally stylized. Avoid fingerprints, rough handmade textures, workshop scenes, macro photography depth-of-field, or photoreal clay imperfections.
Use soft professional studio product lighting: gentle global illumination, warm key light, soft ambient bounce, controlled shadows, and optional warm interior window glow.
Render any water or translucent materials as poured clear resin with smooth transparency, subtle reflections, soft internal depth, and slightly thick stylized edges.
Include small environmental details but keep everything cohesive, simplified, and sculptural. Prioritize clean stylized modeling over photorealistic texture detail.
Overall intent: premium collectible miniature, stylized 3D marketplace presentation, cozy whimsical mood, smooth sculpt clarity, controlled studio rendering, avoid real-world photography aesthetics
```

### 123. 数码泼墨肖像画定制服务

**Author**: [Edraak Tech | إدراك تِك](https://x.com/EdraakTechAi)  **Date**: 2026-02-20  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成插画素描写实风格的垂直数字肖像的提示，带有绘画抽象感，基于上传的照片。它强调面部特征周围的清晰细节和蓬松、随风飘动的头发。

![数码泼墨肖像画定制服务](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771655069002_n5ll6z_HBmziZIWsAAWFwc.jpg)
![数码泼墨肖像画定制服务](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771655069071_0zxku0_HBmziZHWYAEAQUv.jpg)

```
Create a vertical 3:4 digital splashes-and-ink portrait using my photo as the subject, rendered in illustrative sketch realism with painterly abstraction. Frame a medium close-up in a subtle half-quarter turn with a calm but intense, direct gaze; keep crisp linework and highest detail around the eyes, brows, and mouth, while allowing hair strands to stay loose and slightly wind-tossed.
```

### 148. 时尚类 Vlog 风格视频生成提示

**Author**: [空想写真家](https://x.com/KusoPhoto)  **Date**: 2026-02-20  **Language**: ja

> 一个详细的提示，用于使用 Google Veo 3.1 从图像生成视频，重点是一位女性以温暖、亲密和真实的 Vlog 风格展示她的时尚。该提示指定了摄像机角度、灯光、表情和对话，强调自然、高质量的室内视频，不带人工效果。

```
正面を向いた動画風のショットを作成。カメラは顔の高さで固定、被写体の真正面に配置。被写体は姿勢と構図から座っていることが示されている。

構図はシンプルで安定しており、劇的なアングルや目立つカメラの動きはない。照明は[UGCスタイルのショットを考慮した現実的な照明を追加]から。顔ははっきり見える。

被写体の表情は穏やかでリラックスしており、自然なほのかな微笑みを浮かべている。まるでカメラに向かってVlogを語り始めようとしているかのようだ。画質は夜間の屋内で撮影された動画（高画質）を反映しており、フィルター、美化効果、人工的なシャープネス処理は一切施されていない。

空間は個人的な空間として感じられる。ボケはカメラの限界によるもので、人工的な被写界深度効果ではない。全体的な雰囲気は温かく、明るく、親密で、被写体が話し始める直前のリアルなVlogの瞬間を思わせる。

女性のセリフは、「今日のファッションは【ファッションの特徴を追加】がポイントです！」と優しい口調で話しながら服を触っている。最後に笑顔になる。

BGM：Vlog風のファッションの雰囲気に合った音が心地よく流れている。
```

[[Natural Indoor Light]] [[Warm Intimate Lighting]]

```
- If [SUBJECT_TOGGLE] is "OFF": Show only the empty storefront.

- If [SUBJECT_TOGGLE] is "ON": Autonomously add 1-2 characters or a pet that fits the brand's lifestyle.

PHASE 3: DYNAMIC TYPOGRAPHY (CORRECTED).

PHASE 4: VISUAL STYLE.

- Two-tone palette: [BRAND SIGNATURE COLOR] on a pure white background.

- Style: 1950s-60s Retro Line Art. No gradients, no shadows.

TECH SPECS:

Flat 2D vector, 8k resolution, monochrome aesthetic, centered composition.
```

### 179. 阿西莫夫远见分镜概念艺术提示词

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-02-19  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多步骤提示，旨在生成电影级的概念艺术图像（16:9），该图像将场景对角线分割，对比一位远见者（例如：阿西莫夫）的历史工作空间与他们思想的现代实现，并使用对比鲜明的灯光和元素。

![阿西莫夫远见分镜概念艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569162397_s6dgzs_HBT7eY3WoAAIczJ.jpg)
![阿西莫夫远见分镜概念艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569162417_lhsvtu_HBT7eaEaAAA6Gmu.jpg)
![阿西莫夫远见分镜概念艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569162417_hs9og6_HBT7eXXWoAAcWeL.jpg)
![阿西莫夫远见分镜概念艺术提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771569162903_16gf80_HBT7eY2XgAAGJfM.jpg)

```
Do this for Asimov:   1. The Analysis:  
      Analyze Input:   Identify the Visionary's Era (e.g., 1950s) and their Core Predictions (e.g., Robotics, AI).
      Left Side (The Origin):   Construct the room based on the  actual  historical workspace of the person (e.g., Typewriters, cigarette smoke, blueprints, tungsten light).
      Right Side (The Legacy):   Construct the room based on the  modern realization  of their ideas (e.g., Clean server room, holograms, advanced prosthetics, cool LED light).

  2. Composition (The Rift):  
      The Divide:   A diagonal beam of light splits the room.
      The Subject:   The Visionary stands dead center.
         Left Half of Body:  Dressed in period clothing, holding a pen/paper.
         Right Half of Body:  Fading into digital pixels or observing a floating hologram of their invention.
      The Wall:  
         Left Wall:  Covered in pinned sketches and paper notes.
         Right Wall:  A floor-to-ceiling window looking out onto a futuristic city (The world they predicted).

  3. Visual 
      Cohesion:   The perspective lines of the room must match perfectly across the split. A wooden desk on the left might morph into a sleek glass interface on the right.
      Lighting:   Warm/Dusty (Left) vs. Cold/Sterile (Right).

  Output:   ONE image, 16:9 Aspect Ratio, Cinematic Concept Art, Photorealistic.
```

[[Cinematic Concept Art]] [[16:9 Format]]

In the foreground, a smooth sage green oval dining table sits on a pedestal base, surrounded by cream upholstered chairs. ### 199. 远古丛林神庙立体模型收藏品提示

**Author**: [Artingent](https://x.com/artingent)  **Date**: 2026-02-18  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张古代丛林寺庙群立体模型的图像。它详细说明了场景布局（阶梯式寺庙、庭院、苔藓、藤蔓）和所需的风格：一个高级风格化的 3D 收藏微缩模型，由光滑的哑光陶瓷/树脂雕刻而成，具有受控的摄影棚灯光和舒适、异想天开的氛围。

![远古丛林神庙立体模型收藏品提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771483119036_meekzb_HBdpS-hbUAAB3bO.jpg)

```
SCENE:
A larger ancient jungle temple complex featuring a stepped main temple, several surrounding shrine structures, broken ceremonial courtyards, moss-covered staircases, carved statues, fragmented stone walls, and a shallow reflecting pool, all surrounded by dense tropical foliage and vines. Arrange the ruins so the space feels like a compact, layered miniature district with multiple clustered architectural elements, varied heights, and interconnected pathways, filling the platform naturally without empty gaps and reading clearly as a contained archaeological jungle ruin diorama.
STYLE:
Render as a premium stylized 3D collectible miniature diorama on a fully visible, centered self-contained display base, shown from a slightly elevated 3/4 tabletop angle against a clean neutral studio gradient background. Maintain collectible figurine scale and clean display presentation.
All elements should appear sculpted from smooth matte ceramic, painted resin, or stylized polymer with rounded edges, simplified geometry, and slightly exaggerated toy-like proportions. Keep surfaces clean and intentionally stylized. Avoid fingerprints, rough handmade textures, workshop scenes, macro photography depth-of-field, or photoreal clay imperfections.
Use soft professional studio product lighting: gentle global illumination, warm key light, soft ambient bounce, controlled shadows, and optional warm interior window glow.
Render any water or translucent materials as poured clear resin with smooth transparency, subtle reflections, soft internal depth, and slightly thick stylized edges.
Include small environmental details but keep everything cohesive, simplified, and sculptural. Prioritize clean stylized modeling over photorealistic texture detail.
Overall intent: premium collectible miniature, stylized 3D marketplace presentation, cozy whimsical mood, smooth sculpt clarity, controlled studio rendering, avoid real-world photography aesthetics.
```
